  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_912d2118-1887-42bf-9728-957ddcad9317'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer12434998453694333135">No one steps on Archer land. Not if they value their life. But when Meredith Hayes overhears a lethal plot to burn the Archer brothers off their ranch, a twelve-year-old debt compels her to take the risk.<br/><br/>Fourteen years of constant vigilance hardens a man. Yet when Travis Archer confronts a female trespasser with the same vivid blue eyes as the courageous young girl he once</span>
  <span id="freeText12434998453694333135" style="display:none">No one steps on Archer land. Not if they value their life. But when Meredith Hayes overhears a lethal plot to burn the Archer brothers off their ranch, a twelve-year-old debt compels her to take the risk.<br /><br />Fourteen years of constant vigilance hardens a man. Yet when Travis Archer confronts a female trespasser with the same vivid blue eyes as the courageous young girl he once aided, he can't bring himself to send her away. And when an act of sacrifice leaves her injured and her reputation in shreds, gratitude and guilt send him riding to her rescue once again.<br /><br />Four brothers. Four straws. One bride. Despite the fact that Travis is no longer the gallant youth Meredith once dreamed about, she determines to stand by his side against the enemy that threatens them both. But will love ever be hers? Or will Travis always see her merely as a short-straw bride?</span>

<div id="review_349100186" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/349100186" />
    <a title="Regina Jennings" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5508543-regina-jennings"><img alt="Regina Jennings" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442456738p2/5508543.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/349100186?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Regina Jennings" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Regina Jennings" href="/user/show/5508543-regina-jennings">Regina Jennings</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer349100186" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12252882655683856434">Warning - reading this book in public can lead to embarrassment.<br/><br/>I had a doctor appointment recently and was excited to finally have some quiet time to read "Short-Straw Bride". Unfortunately, the waiting room was too quiet. <br/><br/>When young Meredith steals onto Archer land and Travis - the misunderstood and feared hero - comes to her rescue, I was hooked. I was completely engrossed in the story when Meredith, under the impression that she's dreaming, tells the scary Mr. Archer what she really thinks o</span>
  <span id="freeText12252882655683856434" style="display:none">Warning - reading this book in public can lead to embarrassment.<br /><br />I had a doctor appointment recently and was excited to finally have some quiet time to read "Short-Straw Bride". Unfortunately, the waiting room was too quiet. <br /><br />When young Meredith steals onto Archer land and Travis - the misunderstood and feared hero - comes to her rescue, I was hooked. I was completely engrossed in the story when Meredith, under the impression that she's dreaming, tells the scary Mr. Archer what she really thinks of him...and I snorted...snorted loudly earning concerned glances from my waiting-room friends.<br /><br />But I couldn't stop thinking about the story and when I got back to my car I gave into temptation and decided to sit there and read at least one more chapter - after all, the kids were okay without me for just a bit more. One chapter stretched into another...and another. When would Travis figure out that Meredith didn't want him to be SO gentlemanly? Would Crockett, Jim and Neill find brides of their own? (Love their names, by the way.) I was deep into the story when one of my new waiting room acquaintances knocked on the car window to see if I was having car trouble. Busted.<br /><br />Short-Straw Bride is a wonderful story. Travis's confused handling of his bride is endearing. Meredith's hero worship transforms seamlessly into a mature understanding of her husband, without costing him any shine. I don't know if there are subsequent books planned for these entertaining brothers, but sign me up for the petition drive.<br /><br />Well done and highly recommended. Just don't read it with an audience.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12252882655683856434" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24496452-gramy?shelf=five-star-shelf-it-was-amazing">five-star-shelf-it-was-amazing</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2770018354" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15907453271867674717">.<br/>The signs posted on Archer land discouraged trespassers. Fourteen years ago, Meredith Hayes fell instantly in love with Travis Archer, who rescued her after she caught her foot in an animal trap on his land. Slide forward and find Meredith practically engaged, only to discover the man who proposed only wants to marry her for her land and plans to burn down the barn on the Archer's property in order to try to force them to sell their land.<br/><br/>For fourteen years, Travis Archer had been vigilant about</span>
  <span id="freeText15907453271867674717" style="display:none">.<br />The signs posted on Archer land discouraged trespassers. Fourteen years ago, Meredith Hayes fell instantly in love with Travis Archer, who rescued her after she caught her foot in an animal trap on his land. Slide forward and find Meredith practically engaged, only to discover the man who proposed only wants to marry her for her land and plans to burn down the barn on the Archer's property in order to try to force them to sell their land.<br /><br />For fourteen years, Travis Archer had been vigilant about keeping his brothers and himself safe by not allowing people on their land. During most of those same years, Meredith had been hopelessly in love with the kind soul of Travis Archer. Now Meredith chooses once again to dare step foot on Archer land in order to warn them of a dire threat. Their stubborn loyalty leads Meredith and the Archers down a dangerous path and results in an unplanned marriage - ultimately decided on by four brothers drawing straws. The positive range of emotions keeping readers engrossed in this book span from loyalty, gentleness, humor, love - along with negative emotions of anger, deceit, and forcible commands of marriage from a greedy man intent on gobbling up land to sell to the railroad. Faith, trust, and loyalty help these folks overcome the grave peril they had become embroiled in.<br /><br />Available through Kindle Unlimited, this tale stands on its own, but I, along with many readers look forward to more installments about the remaining single brothers. If you want an entertaining read, with a Christian influence, then this is a great choice! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15907453271867674717" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3712396822018115071"><b> NO ONE STEPS ON ARCHER LAND!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393638288i/8744315.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Ok, so, I don't know if it's just me being half-witted or what, but I *still* don't understand the whole Archers-are-not-allowed-off-their-land-and-no-one-is-allowed-on-it-either affair. I mean, I understand how Travis felt responsible for his brothers and did not want anybody trying to coax him into selling his land, but forbidding everyone to even step on his land? I mean, they probably had friends and neighbours, no? Anyway, I didn't bother me that much, and I w</span>
  <span id="freeText3712396822018115071" style="display:none"><b> NO ONE STEPS ON ARCHER LAND!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393638288i/8744315.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Ok, so, I don't know if it's just me being half-witted or what, but I *still* don't understand the whole Archers-are-not-allowed-off-their-land-and-no-one-is-allowed-on-it-either affair. I mean, I understand how Travis felt responsible for his brothers and did not want anybody trying to coax him into selling his land, but forbidding everyone to even step on his land? I mean, they probably had friends and neighbours, no? Anyway, I didn't bother me that much, and I was able to go with it, but I simply thought that the way it was delivered was a bit implausible. <br><br>The mental image of four hot men working on a ranch was not exactly unpleasant, I must say!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393638288i/8744316.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He he he ;) <br><br>The story was overall a lot of fun. Some parts still feel a bit unanswered <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Like, why didn't Cassandra go on with her plan of saying that she was married to Jim, before her parents could force her to marry Mitchell? Why wasn't Meredith worried about her when she left the ranch after she had come to say that her father wanted her to marry Mitchell? There were a few other things too, but I can't think of them for now. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but it had a great plot and wonderful characters. Meredith was a beautiful heroine. She represents the hope and freedom for the Archer brothers, as she teaches Travis to trust God with his life and that of his brothers, and to learn to trust others as well. Meredith is strong, determined and courageous, but she also brings along the sweetness and femininity that was lacking on Archer land. The men aren't used to having a woman with them, or a decent meal and spotless kitchen (one of the brothers is even afraid that his clothes will smell like flowers because a woman is doing the washing! Hahahaha!!).<br><br>Travis was a very likeable hero; tortured, yet very brave and heroic. And not to mention mighty good-looking ;) The love story was cute and heart-warming and I really enjoyed it. The characters were really well-drawn and believable and the writing was just perfect. I had a really hard time putting this book down, and I finished it in 3 days. For the records, that is <i>extremely</i> fast for me!! Karen Witemeyer, I am looking forward to reading more books by you!! <i>Stealing the Preacher</i> will be up next, I can wait to see how Crockett's story will turn out! He was a very fun and likeable character in <i>Short Straw Bride</i>, so I am very excited for the next installment!<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1379820571" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13310605048550268160">What a fun, adventurous and laugh-out-loud story! Karen Witemeyer always deliver with entertaining characters, sigh-worthy romance and danger and suspense and this book definitely did not lack any of these. <br/><br/>The Archer brothers was great. Point. I loved how they interacted with each other, had each others’ back and just generally was a bond not easily broken. Even though I adored all four brothers and Travis with this misplaced burden of responsibility, Crockett was the brother I enjoyed most and</span>
  <span id="freeText13310605048550268160" style="display:none">What a fun, adventurous and laugh-out-loud story! Karen Witemeyer always deliver with entertaining characters, sigh-worthy romance and danger and suspense and this book definitely did not lack any of these. <br /><br />The Archer brothers was great. Point. I loved how they interacted with each other, had each others’ back and just generally was a bond not easily broken. Even though I adored all four brothers and Travis with this misplaced burden of responsibility, Crockett was the brother I enjoyed most and am looking forward to reading more about!<br /><br />Meredith (Meri) - even with her physical disability which sometimes slowed her down, her vibrant, fighting personality was a force to be reckoned with which could not be halted. I enjoyed her interactions with the brothers and her wars with Seth.<br /><br />Even though we saw the bad guy early on and you expect some altercation to happen, the author gave me so many other twists and turns and entertaining events that when the actual event took place, it wasn’t expected in the way it happened. I definitely turned pages to see what will happen.<br /><br />The romance between Travis and Meri was sweet and innocent even though they had a married of convenience. I admired Travis for courting Meri before he expected a ‘real’ marriage.<br /><br />Trust in God’s plans and protection and relying on your neighbours was a strong message which hit close to home.<br /><br />If you never tried this author, I highly recommend her books.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer274538042" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer758844796981705098">Short-Straw Bride is one of my favorites by Karen Witemeyer! I loved all the characters, and really connected to their emotions. The romantic tension is so great; it's one of the best marriage of convenience stories I've read!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer372106872" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer441308060307396434">4.5<br/><br/>I really enjoyed this one. I thought the premise sounded cute, but to be honest I didn’t have the highest expectations. I knew it was a Christian fiction, which sometimes tend to be overly preachy for my taste. So, I was pleasantly surprised by just how much I liked this one. I thought it was really well written, with very likable characters.<br/><br/>Meredith was a fun leading lady. She is feisty, stubborn and kind. She is also fearless and honorable. It was endearing to see her ride onto the Archer r</span>
  <span id="freeText441308060307396434" style="display:none">4.5<br /><br />I really enjoyed this one. I thought the premise sounded cute, but to be honest I didn’t have the highest expectations. I knew it was a Christian fiction, which sometimes tend to be overly preachy for my taste. So, I was pleasantly surprised by just how much I liked this one. I thought it was really well written, with very likable characters.<br /><br />Meredith was a fun leading lady. She is feisty, stubborn and kind. She is also fearless and honorable. It was endearing to see her ride onto the Archer ranch knowing she wouldn’t be welcome, but knowing she had to warn them. Surrounded by four burly men didn’t scare her off, she held her own. I just loved the Archer men. Travis of course was awesome, but I especially loved Crockett. I loved the relationship with the brothers and their loyalty to one another. Travis was a doll; I loved how he was just crazy about Meredith right from the beginning. His attempts to court Meredith were endearing and sweet. Although they really needed to just ditch the brothers and have some alone time! ;)<br /><br />I liked the side story of Jim and Cassie as well, but I’d really love a story about Crockett. He always added a little humor to the situation and was just a likable guy. I want to hear all about his HEA. I admit though, if these boys were truly all alone on the ranch for at least 12 years, they seemed very knowledgeable, mature and I guess normal for having no contact with the outside world. I don’t know how they were all so well adjusted, but I didn’t care because I loved them all. I loved the changes Meredith brought about and just thought the whole story was charming. <br /><br />Content: Clean. Mild Christian elements (praying and scriptures).<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="441308060307396434" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532384685" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11015262708018617234">As a young girl, Meredith Hayes made the mistake of stumbling onto restricted Archer land. And into a steel trap that left her with a permanent limp. As well as a permanent weakness for the young man who pulled her out of that trap, Travis Archer.<br/><br/>Years later, Meredith is now a young woman, expected to marry for the good of her aunt and uncle’s financial security. But when Meredith overhears her espoused suitor plotting to burn down the Archer barn, she eschews family loyalty. And sneaks onto Arc</span>
  <span id="freeText11015262708018617234" style="display:none">As a young girl, Meredith Hayes made the mistake of stumbling onto restricted Archer land. And into a steel trap that left her with a permanent limp. As well as a permanent weakness for the young man who pulled her out of that trap, Travis Archer.<br /><br />Years later, Meredith is now a young woman, expected to marry for the good of her aunt and uncle’s financial security. But when Meredith overhears her espoused suitor plotting to burn down the Archer barn, she eschews family loyalty. And sneaks onto Archer land in order to warn the man who rescued her so many years ago.<br /><br />A decision that results in the dissolution of her near engagement, a dire threat from her father, and the startling possibility of a future with the man she has always loved.<br /><br />But will HE love the idea of being forced to marry HER? <br /><br />Sheer wonderful romantic fluff! So much fun. I especially enjoyed Travis’s relationship with his brothers and his inner conflict as he tried to balance his family’s history of seclusion opposite Meredith’s uncageable spirit.<br /></span>

<div id="review_366938655" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/366938655" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4075354-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606221712p2/4075354.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/366938655?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/4075354-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17186535-short-straw-bride">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=kindle-read">kindle-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=cfd-bookclub">cfd-bookclub</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=abc-challenges">abc-challenges</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=christian-fiction">christian-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4075354-beth?shelf=favorites-2013">favorites-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer366938655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9041541629831919574">I adored every minute that I spent reading Short-Straw Bride. The tension and interaction between the main character, Meredith, and the male lead, Travis, was swoon-worth and so sweet. Travis was protective, stubborn and sweet and Meredith was both brave and vulnerable at the same time. Their relationship progressed in a really heartfelt way, and watching their relationship develop after their "short-straw" wedding tugged at my heart. The supporting characters, especially the other 3 Archers bro</span>
  <span id="freeText9041541629831919574" style="display:none">I adored every minute that I spent reading Short-Straw Bride. The tension and interaction between the main character, Meredith, and the male lead, Travis, was swoon-worth and so sweet. Travis was protective, stubborn and sweet and Meredith was both brave and vulnerable at the same time. Their relationship progressed in a really heartfelt way, and watching their relationship develop after their "short-straw" wedding tugged at my heart. The supporting characters, especially the other 3 Archers brothers, were endearing. I like how the story emphasized familial love and not just romantic love.<br /><br />The plot flowed so well. The story line itself could have been predictable, but Witemeyer through a twist in there that definitely gave the story it's own unique twist. It was adventurous, exciting and a little on the tense side, which I loved. Witemeyer does a great job with intermingling details about the Archer's past as well as Meredith's past without resulting to exposition, and they really added depth to the story. There were some parts that I found a little cheesy, but for the most part, I didn't mind it.<br /><br />I definitely recommend Short Straw Bride for readers who like romantic stories with some adventure thrown in the mix.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9041541629831919574" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2721078323389521270">★★★★½ (This is a review of the audiobook.) You know a narrator is good when a secondary character starts speaking and you know who it is right away, without other clues. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7510521.Pilar_Witherspoon' title='Pilar Witherspoon' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pilar Witherspoon</a> gives such a performance in this wonderful, sweet romance. Her enunciation, pace, and tones are all perfect for every character. I’ll definitely look for more of her readings.<br/><br/>What a lovely romance. It is certainly “one-foot-on-the-floor” – but still, there is plenty of heat between the hero and heroine. And the</span>
  <span id="freeText2721078323389521270" style="display:none">★★★★½ (This is a review of the audiobook.) You know a narrator is good when a secondary character starts speaking and you know who it is right away, without other clues. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7510521.Pilar_Witherspoon" title="Pilar Witherspoon" rel="nofollow noopener">Pilar Witherspoon</a> gives such a performance in this wonderful, sweet romance. Her enunciation, pace, and tones are all perfect for every character. I’ll definitely look for more of her readings.<br /><br />What a lovely romance. It is certainly “one-foot-on-the-floor” – but still, there is plenty of heat between the hero and heroine. And there’s plenty of action in the storyline. I loved Travis and Meredith’s love story. Both characters come alive in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3114906.Karen_Witemeyer" title="Karen Witemeyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Karen Witemeyer</a>’s book. While I’ve certainly noticed her books before, due to the lovely covers, I’ve never read anything by her. That’s about to change; I definitely will be reading more of her work. Also, the religious aspect of the book is not shoved down your throat, but done in a heartwarming, realistic way for time, place, and situation.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578367586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13857702138335020047">So I finally got a chance to read Short Straw Bride and Oh. My. Goodness. Karen never disappoints me, her novels are pure perfection and I just adored this sweet story. It seems all of Karen's books that I read end up on my favourites shelf. I absolutely loved this story and I'll have a more full review to come soon!<br/><br/><br/>UPDATE 04/13/2015:<br/><br/>Short Straw Bride is absolutely on my BEST of 2015 list and snuck to the top of it. Short Straw Bride is my third Karen Witemeyer novel and reminded me why Karen is</span>
  <span id="freeText13857702138335020047" style="display:none">So I finally got a chance to read Short Straw Bride and Oh. My. Goodness. Karen never disappoints me, her novels are pure perfection and I just adored this sweet story. It seems all of Karen's books that I read end up on my favourites shelf. I absolutely loved this story and I'll have a more full review to come soon!<br /><br /><br />UPDATE 04/13/2015:<br /><br />Short Straw Bride is absolutely on my BEST of 2015 list and snuck to the top of it. Short Straw Bride is my third Karen Witemeyer novel and reminded me why Karen is one of my favourite historical authors. Karen's writing is so engaging and historically accurate that it sucks you in from the first page. I never put this book down as I started it at midnight and did not finish until 3 am. Short Straw Bride is Travis and Meri's story and what a story it was. Good-looking Cowboys, swoon-worthy romance, and life-altering conflict, for me is the perfect recipe for the perfect read. I also love that Karen is not afraid to show religious conviction and Scripture in her novels. Something I have noticed as of late that is lacking a bit. This is Christian fiction after all and we are commanded to preach the Gospel and share Jesus in every aspect of our lives. Thank you Karen. And oh the romance...it was so good and full of tension. Just one of the many ingredients of this story that kept me turning the page. I will absolutely purchasing the three novels previous to this one sometime this year! I suggest you pick up this book and once you do you won't want to put it down for any reason.<br /><br /><br /><br />UPDATE 03/23/17: Yeah...it's still amazing and I still swoon over Travis Archer. </span>

<div id="review_351189509" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Abby Moreland" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6640251-abby-moreland"><img alt="Abby Moreland" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393636015p2/6640251.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/351189509?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Abby Moreland" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Abby Moreland" href="/user/show/6640251-abby-moreland">Abby Moreland</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351189509" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer192717960470034161">holy cow, I loved this book. definitely surprised me. honestly, I don't really know what I was expecting as I sat down to start this book, but I don't believe I was expecting to fall in love! already have another book by Whitemeyer on hold at the library. hehe.<br/>rarely ever do I start the first chapter of a book and immediately get sucked in. rarely, rarely, rarely. (my standards are pretty high for books, if you couldn't tell. hah.) but this book had me captured by the first few paragraphs. even </span>
  <span id="freeText192717960470034161" style="display:none">holy cow, I loved this book. definitely surprised me. honestly, I don't really know what I was expecting as I sat down to start this book, but I don't believe I was expecting to fall in love! already have another book by Whitemeyer on hold at the library. hehe.<br />rarely ever do I start the first chapter of a book and immediately get sucked in. rarely, rarely, rarely. (my standards are pretty high for books, if you couldn't tell. hah.) but this book had me captured by the first few paragraphs. even with family here traveling from 2,000 miles away, I read this book in two days. didn't even have time to record my progress on goodreads. that's such a nerdy thing to say.<br />Whitemeyer's writing style had me captured as well. I can't even place what it is... it's like I kept reading things in the way I would write it. which made me excited. the writing is fairly simple, but still keeps all the good stuff in there. I also found that I rarely encountered a cliche saying... ya know like the "raked his hand through his hair" or the "remorse coursed through his body." the kinda thing found in historical fiction romance books. hah.<br />the plot was pretty predictable... not terribly so. but enough to not be surprised by the ending. of course it's kind of like that with love stories - they're going to fall in love and be happy the rest of their life. that's just the way it is and if that changed I would be sad. I like happy endings. it wasn't boring to read at all, though... and of course all the subplots kept me guessing.<br />if you like love stories, I would definitely recommend this book. it's really sweet and original.<br />one thing that did sort of annoy me though, was Merideth's change of mood so often. maybe it's just cause she's a girl. ;) but it seemed she would believe Travis loved her in the morning, then by night think he'd never want to see her again. anyone else find that a tad annoying?<br />the book has lots of action, lots of suspense, and lots of bad guys to dislike. awesome. <br />overall it was a great book - and hey, I rated it 5 stars! only the best of the best get a 5 star. I found a new book that I'll probably re-read, and found an amazing author whose other books are at the top of my book list.<br />bravo, Whitemeyer!</span>
  <a data-text-id="192717960470034161" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4813774738617981067">Age Appropriate For: 15 and up for marital themes<br/><br/>Best for Ages: 18 and up<br/><br/>This book had been sitting on my Kindle for a few months. Several of my friends kept raving about Karen Witemeyer, so I decided to give her a try thinking it would be a nice, light, one-time read. Boy, was I in for a big surprise.<br/><br/>It was so refreshing to have a strong Christian message without feeling preachy. I know it is hard for many authors to find that happy medium. If they want some pointers, study Karen Witemeyer. Her</span>
  <span id="freeText4813774738617981067" style="display:none">Age Appropriate For: 15 and up for marital themes<br /><br />Best for Ages: 18 and up<br /><br />This book had been sitting on my Kindle for a few months. Several of my friends kept raving about Karen Witemeyer, so I decided to give her a try thinking it would be a nice, light, one-time read. Boy, was I in for a big surprise.<br /><br />It was so refreshing to have a strong Christian message without feeling preachy. I know it is hard for many authors to find that happy medium. If they want some pointers, study Karen Witemeyer. Her messages are woven seamlessly into the story, yet make you feel stronger in your faith. I don't know how she does it, but I plan to study her work.<br /><br />Travis? I wish I could marry a guy like him. He was human, had faults, but had a strong, sustaining faith. He has respect for Meredith and other women and is a real leader. I love how he develops.<br /><br />Finally! A book set in Texas that actually sounds like Texas. So many books sound like Hollywood's version of Texas, which, if you live here, is far from the truth. Witemeyer is a Texan so that helps, but she did an excellent job of representing the state I call home.<br /><br />This book is for older reads due to the fact most of it takes place after they are married. There were a couple of conversations that might make younger and sensitive readers squirm a little, but nothing is described at all. I am pretty sensitive, but nothing talked about took away from the enjoyment of the story.<br /><br />I highly recommend this book to those who love romance, cowboy stories, and faith-building fiction.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4813774738617981067" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText16968022678054894958" style="display:none">4.55 stars - mild pg13<br /><br />Great, fun story of romantic and family love. Bit of adventure. Trusting God. Wonderful secondary characters (loved Crockett and Moses). {Where do I find one of these ranches full of smokin' hot Godly men just waiting for the right woman??? <span id="freeTextContainer1292983708992511071">I heard Karen say that the musical Seven Brides For Seven Brothers inspired the idea for this story. As it happens, I was charmed by the movie and likewise very much charmed by Karen's take on the premise.<br/><br/>In Short-Straw Bride, four brawny cowboy brothers all live sequestered away on their ranch. None have left its boundaries for years and years. Then a woman is dropped into their midst and their carefully ordered lives are turned upside down.   <span id="freeText1292983708992511071" style="display:none">I heard Karen say that the musical Seven Brides For Seven Brothers inspired the idea for this story. As it happens, I was charmed by the movie and likewise very much charmed by Karen's take on the premise.<br /><br />In Short-Straw Bride, four brawny cowboy brothers all live sequestered away on their ranch. None have left its boundaries for years and years. Then a woman is dropped into their midst and their carefully ordered lives are turned upside down. (Which is lots of fun to watch). :) <br /><br />Karen is such a talented author! Her books are regularly nominated for industry awards and she recently snagged the Holt medallion. After reading Short-Straw Bride I can clearly see why. This novel is well written and carefully crafted by an author with a gift for story telling. <br /><br />Oh, and I'm a sucker -- SUCKER! -- for stories where the hero and heroine first meet as kids. Loved the prologue! <br /><br /> </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1833477662" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16539937931284264431">It's difficult to find good Christian romance authors, but I think that Whitemeyer did a fantastic job. <br/><br/>I feel like we get a lot of couples who just get married because the girl and the guy love each other. One of the things I like about this book was that the guy and the girl knew that they had feelings for each other, yet they weren't a hundred percent sure that God wanted them to marry. They wanted to make sure that they were doing God's will. And that, to me, is far more realistic.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_767912501" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/767912501" />
    <a title="Maria" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19799133-maria"><img alt="Maria" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1382981396p2/19799133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/767912501?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria" href="/user/show/19799133-maria">Maria</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17186535-short-straw-bride">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19799133-maria?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19799133-maria?shelf=christian-fiction">christian-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer767912501" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer678764777490795834">Twelve years ago Travis Archer saved Meredith Hayes’ life by freeing her from a steel trap. Since then she has always thought he was the man of her dreams and secretly loved him, despite they were both very young and he was considered a dangerous boy. Now, after many years without seeing each other, it is her turn to save his life and his brothers’ as well. But once at their ranch her life will change forever. Her reputation is in danger and the only solution is to marry one of the Archer brothe</span>
  <span id="freeText678764777490795834" style="display:none">Twelve years ago Travis Archer saved Meredith Hayes’ life by freeing her from a steel trap. Since then she has always thought he was the man of her dreams and secretly loved him, despite they were both very young and he was considered a dangerous boy. Now, after many years without seeing each other, it is her turn to save his life and his brothers’ as well. But once at their ranch her life will change forever. Her reputation is in danger and the only solution is to marry one of the Archer brothers. Who will be the future husband? To resolve the problem (although it is not at all a problem for one of them), the four brothers decide to draw straws and after the contest the most exciting journey begins.<br /><br />Have you ever had that feeling you would love a book from the very first pages? I have. And this is one of those cases. I loved this story! And I am sure of that because the characters are still lingering in my mind and in my heart, and I have the impression they will stay forever!<br /><br />I knew I would love everything from the first time Ms. Witemeyer gave voice to Meredith’s thoughts. She is a wonderful heroine. She is strong, determined and yet fragile. Her need of protection along with her boldness are so perfectly depicted I adored every single word used to tell her personality and actions. It is predictable and almost expected that a girl like that must have a remarkable hero. Travis Archer is a great hero!! He has definitely gained a special place on my list of swoon-worthy heroes! Although he is distrustful and reluctant to open up his property gate and his heart to the world, he is so loving and caring and protective it was so beautiful reading about him... I clearly envy Meredith!<br /><br />Furthermore, I love the entire Archer family. Each brother has something special inside of them that gives something more to the story. Crockett is the educated brother who loves to tease Travis, Jim is the reserved, stoic one and Neill is the youngest and always eager to enter the fray. The family is paramount for the brothers and they are willing to give up their lives for each other. They always say “Archers stand together, no matter what” and I loved how they soon welcome Meredith to their family. Even if at the beginning they do not trust a woman in their home (and there are some funny scenes that prove that), she becomes suddenly part of them all and they immediately show her their protectiveness. I am looking forward to the second book of this series, “Stealing the preacher”, to know other aspects of this amazing family. <br /><br />Lastly, a special mention to the cover, is that not cute?! I love it! And it clearly explains the basis of the story: the short-straw contest that will be of great importance for one of the brother. It is easy to guess who will be the lucky guy but I will not spoil anything because it is a real pleasure to see how things go for each of the characters. In this book you will find not only romance but also adventure and an unexpected twist that will strongly engage you, and I can tell you will not want to stop reading until you reach the end. I heartily recommend it!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="678764777490795834" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2486670710" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2486670710" />
    <a title="Alaina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50620706-alaina"><img alt="Alaina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451325817p2/50620706.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2486670710?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alaina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alaina" href="/user/show/50620706-alaina">Alaina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50620706-alaina?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2486670710" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18200078984483597786"><b>Cute audio book.</b><br/><br/><i>Short-Straw Bride</i> was one of those random audio books that I picked from my KU's romance package. Now if I'm being completely honest, it wasn't a bad read. Nope, it was pretty enjoyable and I was highly interested to see how it was all going to play out.<br/><br/>In this book, you will meet Meredith and Travis. When they first met, Meredith was sort of trespassing on his land. Of course everyone knows not to step onto it but she was kind of getting bullied and a boy threw her lunch pail in</span>
  <span id="freeText18200078984483597786" style="display:none"><b>Cute audio book.</b><br /><br /><i>Short-Straw Bride</i> was one of those random audio books that I picked from my KU's romance package. Now if I'm being completely honest, it wasn't a bad read. Nope, it was pretty enjoyable and I was highly interested to see how it was all going to play out.<br /><br />In this book, you will meet Meredith and Travis. When they first met, Meredith was sort of trespassing on his land. Of course everyone knows not to step onto it but she was kind of getting bullied and a boy threw her lunch pail into it. So the daring girl that she is, walked right onto it with no fear. Well, that plan went sour real quick because she ended up being stuck in a trap that eventually gave her a bad leg. <br /><br />From that moment, they've sort of had this spark about them. Meredith had always dreamed about being married to Travis.. whereas, he didn't really know it was her until the day she trespassed right back onto his land. It was fate - but really she was warning him about her soon-to-be-ex-fiancee trying to buy his land by burning it. <br /><br />Of course there's a bunch of backstabbing in this book and a ton of betrayal from family members. However, I'm not going to talk about that. Nope, I'm going to talk about the little teasing moments between these two. Heck even the little sexual tension here and there. Okay, so these two ended up getting married but they never really acted like husband and wife. They haven't even done the deed yet - gasp! <br /><br />Travis and Meredith were freaking adorable together. It frustrated me that he wanted to court her even though she was his wife and all... and I'm like, I feel your frustration girl! Just kiss him. Eventually, towards the end I might add, they finally come to terms that they are both madly in love with each other. This conclusion also leads to them finally wanting to act like husband and wife. PRAISE BABY JESUS!<br /><br />Overall, it was a very cute audio.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18200078984483597786" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2229570964" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2229570964" />
    <a title="Rebekah Brown" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69590311-rebekah-brown"><img alt="Rebekah Brown" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534347247p2/69590311.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2229570964?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rebekah Brown" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rebekah Brown" href="/user/show/69590311-rebekah-brown">Rebekah Brown</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69590311-rebekah-brown?shelf=50-states-2018-challenge">50-states-2018-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69590311-rebekah-brown?shelf=abc-s-2018-challenge">abc-s-2018-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69590311-rebekah-brown?shelf=library-books-2018-challenge">library-books-2018-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69590311-rebekah-brown?shelf=1800-s-historical-fiction">1800-s-historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69590311-rebekah-brown?shelf=library-books">library-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69590311-rebekah-brown?shelf=around-the-world-2018-challenge">around-the-world-2018-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2229570964" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8659223336970803120">As a huge fan of Karen Witemeyer, I was eager to read her acclaimed Short-Straw Bride. I have heard many say that of all her novels, Short-Straw Bride is their favorite. With that said, I expected this book to be my favorite (funny how that works), and even though I enjoyed it... it is not on my top 3 list for Witemeyer's novels. <br/><br/>Short- Straw Bride's main characters are well developed and each have their moments to shine in the story. Travis, the oldest of the Archer brothers, has been taking ca</span>
  <span id="freeText8659223336970803120" style="display:none">As a huge fan of Karen Witemeyer, I was eager to read her acclaimed Short-Straw Bride. I have heard many say that of all her novels, Short-Straw Bride is their favorite. With that said, I expected this book to be my favorite (funny how that works), and even though I enjoyed it... it is not on my top 3 list for Witemeyer's novels. <br /><br />Short- Straw Bride's main characters are well developed and each have their moments to shine in the story. Travis, the oldest of the Archer brothers, has been taking care of his brothers since his father's passing during the time he was coming of age. Travis has an extreme sense of guilt and duty that clouds his ideas, thoughts, and actions. But all of this is to change when a girl from his past reappears. As a young girl, Meredith was caught on Archer land (#1 rule of a No-No!), Travis' compassion wins out over his duty, and he helps Meredith from a trap she accidentally stepped in. Since that day, Meredith has idolized Travis, and secretly wishes she would meet his again one day.<br /><br />Meredith, is a passionate young woman that thinks for herself and puts others needs above her own. When Travis and Meredith reunite years later, sparks begin to fly immediately. The banter between the two and the snide comments from the other Archer brothers provided a funny and heartwarming read. Travis is used to everyone taking his orders and not questioning his commands. "Uh, oh"...Meredith is the opposite of a docile female. <br /><br />What bugged me? Meredith's constant, he loves me..he loves me not battle happening in her mind. Even though she is a young woman, the back and forth of acting on her emotions I found to be a little annoying. Cassie and Jim's "relationship" was also quite interesting. I have never experienced love at first sight, but relationships built on mutual respect, trust, and friendship. I would have liked to see more of their relationship development in the story, their component felt rushed to me. Perhaps we will discover their romance in Archer Brothers #2? <br /><br />Short-Straw Bride is a fast paced read that engages the reader by delivering a balanced amount of romance, action, and inner conflict. I'm off to my next Witemeyer novel!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8659223336970803120" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_339123415" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/339123415" />
    <a title="Katie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2790490-katie"><img alt="Katie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442500886p2/2790490.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/339123415?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie" href="/user/show/2790490-katie">Katie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer339123415" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6235822582134967610">First posted on my blog, <a href='http://katie-mccurdy.blogspot.com/2012/06/once-again-karen-witemeyer-has-penned.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Legacy of a Writer</a>.<br/><br/>Once again, Karen Witemeyer has penned another wonderful read!! Short-Straw Bride pricks your interest with the prologue and by the second chapter, I was captivated. After reading two other books by Witemeyer, I know to expect a book that will entertain, enthrall, and warm your heart all at the same time—and she’s done again with Short-Straw Bride!<br/><br/>I really enjoyed getting to know Meredith and the Archer men. The story behind why the Archer’s are so fea</span>
  <span id="freeText6235822582134967610" style="display:none">First posted on my blog, <a href="http://katie-mccurdy.blogspot.com/2012/06/once-again-karen-witemeyer-has-penned.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Legacy of a Writer</a>.<br /><br />Once again, Karen Witemeyer has penned another wonderful read!! Short-Straw Bride pricks your interest with the prologue and by the second chapter, I was captivated. After reading two other books by Witemeyer, I know to expect a book that will entertain, enthrall, and warm your heart all at the same time—and she’s done again with Short-Straw Bride!<br /><br />I really enjoyed getting to know Meredith and the Archer men. The story behind why the Archer’s are so feared and never leave their land was very interesting and well woven into the story. I always know that Witemeyer will have something different an unqiue in her books—character quirk, interesting predicament or place—and this one is no exception. Even after finishing the book, I am still stuck on Archer’s land.<br /><br />Watching Travis and Meredith learn and grow to love each other after marriage was so memorable. You can’t help but cheer for them as the book progresses. The romance between the two is warm and funny—a few scenes even get the blood pumping! (Though nothing ever too descriptive, in my opinion. No worries! ;-)<br /><br />Short-Straw Bride had a very fun and different story plot from what I have been reading recently—so a delightful change of pace for me! All in all, I loved it. Each book that I have read by Witemeyer, I have fully and completely enjoyed, and Short-Straw Bride is no exception.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6235822582134967610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1900985040" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1900985040" />
    <a title="Amanda G. Stevens" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9779665-amanda-g-stevens"><img alt="Amanda G. Stevens" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442981901p2/9779665.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1900985040?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda G. Stevens" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda G. Stevens" href="/user/show/9779665-amanda-g-stevens">Amanda G. Stevens</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1900985040" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer915484043911349006">Romance in any form is quite the genre departure for me, but this book is downright huggable, and I'm glad I gave it a chance. Three smiling stars for two characters whose marriage is easy to root for because they're simply so endearing. As is the book itself. The plot goes a little haywire by the end, and the directness ("telling-not-showing") of the style distracted me for the first few chapters until I acclimated to it, but I'm glad I kept reading. I love Travis's protector streak, his stubbo</span>
  <span id="freeText915484043911349006" style="display:none">Romance in any form is quite the genre departure for me, but this book is downright huggable, and I'm glad I gave it a chance. Three smiling stars for two characters whose marriage is easy to root for because they're simply so endearing. As is the book itself. The plot goes a little haywire by the end, and the directness ("telling-not-showing") of the style distracted me for the first few chapters until I acclimated to it, but I'm glad I kept reading. I love Travis's protector streak, his stubbornness and insecurities and how these elements of his personality both feed and balance each other. I love Meredith's assertiveness that never falls into annoying "spunk" or unrealistic modern-woman behavior. I love how determined both of them are to honor God in an unexpected marriage. Simply an adorable story.</span>
  <a data-text-id="915484043911349006" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_597071670" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/597071670" />
    <a title="Andrea Cox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16407549-andrea-cox"><img alt="Andrea Cox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1358113989p2/16407549.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/597071670?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andrea Cox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andrea Cox" href="/user/show/16407549-andrea-cox">Andrea Cox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=1870s">1870s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=2020-cfd-pick-genre">2020-cfd-pick-genre</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=weather-rain">weather-rain</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=adventure">adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=kidnappings">kidnappings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=westerns">westerns</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=cowboys-and-ranches">cowboys-and-ranches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16407549-andrea-cox?shelf=1880s">1880s</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer597071670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10573447026936699288">What a fun story! I enjoyed the Seven Brides for Seven Brothers feel of this one. It was entertaining from start to finish, and I loved the spunkiness of not only Meredith but also the four Archer brothers. As usual, this Witemeyer book kept me riveted, laughing, and cruising through the pages. I can hardly wait to start the next book in this series.<br/><br/>Content: one expletive<br/></span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('heJWnzsqdV8anA4DI5wUre3QA/Abf9Lq0gSm/Pfhii32jJmEmbKVMI6f9mCrkv9CMeJjp9/WznJsJbK/e3zM9w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer3786893222426700219">For those who love to smile as they read, bestselling author Karen Witemeyer offers warmhearted historical romance with a flair for humor, feisty heroines, and swoon-worthy Texas heroes. A transplant from California, Karen came to Texas for college, met a cowboy disguised as a computer nerd, married him, and never left the state that had become home. <br/><br/>Winner of the National Reader's Choice Award, H</span>
  <span id="freeText3786893222426700219" style="display:none">For those who love to smile as they read, bestselling author Karen Witemeyer offers warmhearted historical romance with a flair for humor, feisty heroines, and swoon-worthy Texas heroes. A transplant from California, Karen came to Texas for college, met a cowboy disguised as a computer nerd, married him, and never left the state that had become home. <br /><br />Winner of the National Reader's Choice Award, HOLT Medallion, ACFW Carol Award, Inspirational Reader's Choice Award, and a finalist for both the RITA and Christy Awards, Karen is a firm believer in the power of happy endings. . . and ice cream. She also loves to reward her readers. Every month she gives away two inspirational historical novels to someone from her newsletter list and offers substantial bonus content on her website. To learn more about Karen and her books, or to join her subscriber list, please visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.karenwitemeyer.com">www.karenwitemeyer.com</a>.<br /></span>
